[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1256[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1257[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mWINPR_ASSERT[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1258[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1259[0m[39m:   [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mx509_validate_subject_aternative_names[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert->x509[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1260[0m[39m:   [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn FALSE;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibfreerdp/crypto/x509_utils.h:[0m[1;36m61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m61[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:     [0m[39mFREERDP_LOCAL BOOL [0m[1;35mx509_validate_subject_aternative_names[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst X509* [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability in `x509_validate_subject_aternative_names` [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlibfreerdp/crypto/x509_utils.[0m[1;92mc:433[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m474[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m stems from a fundamental mismatch between [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer allocation and data copying:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m452[0m[39m**: Allocates buffer using `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_get0_data[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` counts bytes until the first null byte[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m in the crash case → allocates [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m457[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[39m**: Copies data using `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_length[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns the actual ASN.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m string length regardless of embedded nulls[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m in the crash case → attempts to write [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m bytes[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Result**: Heap buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes allocated, [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m bytes written[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Additional Issues[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Missing null terminator**: `memcpy` doesn't add [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m, breaking `[0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich expects null-terminated strings[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Wrong return value**: Always returns TRUE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m473[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ignoring validation [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailures[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Incorrect pattern**: Should use `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` like other functions in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe codebase[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Pattern Analysis[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase has established patterns for handling ASN.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m strings:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Correct Pattern** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused in `extract_string`, `x509_utils_get_common_name`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned char* utf8_string = NULL;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint length = [0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&utf8_string, asn1_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Error handling[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Use utf8_string [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull-terminated[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mutf8_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Works**:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Handles all ASN.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m encodings [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUTF8String, BMPString, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Converts to null-terminated UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Returns actual length[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No embedded nulls in UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m output[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Replace Manual Allocation with ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: libfreerdp/crypto/x509_utils.c, function [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`x509_validate_subject_aternative_names` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m433[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m474[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Replace the allocation and copy logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m452[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdns_name = [0m[1;35mmalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_get0_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mgen_name->d.dNSName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    goto end;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_get0_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mgen_name->d.dNSName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mgen_name->d.dNSName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned char* dns_name_raw = NULL;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint length = [0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&dns_name_raw, gen_name->d.dNSName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[32m([0m[32m)[0m[32m failed for DNS name: %s"[0m[39m,[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mERR_error_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mERR_get_error[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    result = FALSE;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    goto end;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdns_name = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mdns_name_raw;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Update the cleanup logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m461[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m465[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace all instances of:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdns_name = NULL;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Fix the return value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m473[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturn TRUE;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturn result;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Add cleanup in the end label [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m471[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBefore `sk_GENERAL_NAME_pop_free`, add:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Update variable declaration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m436[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar *dns_name = NULL;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo match the new usage pattern throughout the function.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Complete Fixed Implementation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fixed function should follow this structure:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBOOL [0m[1;35mx509_validate_subject_aternative_names[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst X509* cert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mSTACK_OF[0m[1;39m([0m[39mGENERAL_NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m *san_names = NULL;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    int i, count;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    unsigned char *dns_name = NULL;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    BOOL result = TRUE;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Get Subject Alternative Names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSAN[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    san_names = [0m[1;35mX509_get_ext_d2i[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert, NID_subject_alt_name, NULL, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!san_names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        goto end;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    count = [0m[1;35msk_GENERAL_NAME_num[0m[1;39m([0m[39msan_names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < count; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        GENERAL_NAME *gen_name = [0m[1;35msk_GENERAL_NAME_value[0m[1;39m([0m[39msan_names, i[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgen_name->type == GEN_DNS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Convert ASN1 string to UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            int length = [0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&dns_name, gen_name->d.dNSName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mWLog_ERR[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTAG, [0m[32m"ASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[32m([0m[32m)[0m[32m failed for DNS name: %s"[0m[39m,[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                         [0m[1;35mERR_error_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mERR_get_error[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                result = FALSE;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                goto end;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                dns_name = NULL;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                result = FALSE;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                goto end;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            dns_name = NULL;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mend:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35msk_GENERAL_NAME_pop_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39msan_names, GENERAL_NAME_free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return result;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Established Codebase Patterns**: Uses the same `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern as `[0m[1;35mextract_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m297[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `[0m[1;35mx509_utils_get_common_name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m859[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and other functions[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fixes All Issues**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates buffer overflow by using OpenSSL's safe conversion[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures null-terminated strings for `[0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Returns correct validation result[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Proper error handling with logging[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Existing Logic**: Preserves the validation behavior - still iterates[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough DNS SANs and calls `[0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on each[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only modifies the vulnerable function, no API changes [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeded[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Correct Memory Management**: Uses `[0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for OpenSSL-allocated [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory, following codebase conventions[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Heap Buffer Overflow**: `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` allocates the correct buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize based on converted UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m length, not [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Null Termination**: The converted UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m string is properly null-terminated[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Return Value**: Now returns `result` instead of always TRUE[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Error Handling**: Checks for conversion errors and logs them appropriately[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Certificate validation chain**: Unchanged - function still called from [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfreerdp_rsa_from_x509[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m1259[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Validation behavior**: Same - validates all DNS SANs, fails on first invalid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **API compatibility**: Function signature unchanged, still declared in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mx509_utils.h:[0m[1;36m61[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Test compatibility**: No changes to test harness or fuzzing logic[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Performance: `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` has minimal overhead compared to the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevious [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbroken[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m approach[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Error messages: Now logs conversion failures, which is beneficial for debugging[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Breaking Changes**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Same function signature[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Same return value semantics [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTRUE = valid, FALSE = invalid[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Same external behavior for valid certificates[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Properly rejects malformed certificates that previously caused crashes[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix follows the exact pattern used in:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mextract_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mx509_utils.[0m[1;92mc:297[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m302[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m308[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mx509_utils_get_common_name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mx509_utils.[0m[1;92mc:859[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m867[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mobject_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mx509_utils.[0m[1;92mc:375[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m383[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these functions demonstrate the correct way to extract and handle ASN.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m strings[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the FreeRDP codebase.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
